// FILE: artifacts/bot-manager/vite.config.ts
============================================================

import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
import tailwindcss from "@tailwindcss/vite";
import path from "path";
import runtimeErrorOverlay from "@replit/vite-plugin-runtime-error-modal";

const rawPort = process.env.PORT;

if (!rawPort) {
  throw new Error(
    "PORT environment variable is required but was not provided.",
  );
}

const port = Number(rawPort);

if (Number.isNaN(port) || port <= 0) {
  throw new Error(`Invalid PORT value: "${rawPort}"`);
}

const basePath = process.env.BASE_PATH;

if (!basePath) {
  throw new Error(
    "BASE_PATH environment variable is required but was not provided.",
  );
}

export default defineConfig({
  base: basePath,
  plugins: [
    react(),
    tailwindcss(),
    runtimeErrorOverlay(),
    ...(process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" &&
    process.env.REPL_ID !== undefined
      ? [
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-cartographer").then((m) =>
            m.cartographer({
              root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, ".."),
            }),
          ),
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-dev-banner").then((m) =>
            m.devBanner(),
          ),
        ]
      : []),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      "@": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "src"),
      "@assets": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "..", "..", "attached_assets"),
    },
    dedupe: ["react", "react-dom"],
  },
  root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname),
  build: {
    outDir: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "dist/public"),
    emptyOutDir: true,
  },
  server: {
    port,
    strictPort: true,
    host: "0.0.0.0",
    allowedHosts: true,
    fs: {
      strict: true,
    },
  },
  preview: {
    port,
    host: "0.0.0.0",
    allowedHosts: true,
  },
});

// FILE: artifacts/bot-manager/src/App.tsx
============================================================

import { Switch, Route, Router as WouterRouter } from "wouter";
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/toaster";
import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
import NotFound from "@/pages/not-found";
import Dashboard from "@/pages/dashboard";
import AddBot from "@/pages/add-bot";
import BotDetail from "@/pages/bot-detail";
import SelfbotsPage from "@/pages/selfbots";

const queryClient = new QueryClient();

function Router() {
  return (
    <Switch>
      <Route path="/" component={Dashboard} />
      <Route path="/bots/new" component={AddBot} />
      <Route path="/bots/:botId" component={BotDetail} />
      <Route path="/selfbots" component={SelfbotsPage} />
      <Route component={NotFound} />
    </Switch>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <TooltipProvider>
        <WouterRouter base={import.meta.env.BASE_URL.replace(/\/$/, "")}>
          <Router />
        </WouterRouter>
        <Toaster />
      </TooltipProvider>
    </QueryClientProvider>
  );
}

export default App;

// FILE: artifacts/bot-manager/src/components/bot/logs-tab.tsx
============================================================

import React from "react";
import { useListBotLogs } from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
import { FileText } from "lucide-react";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";

export function LogsTab({ botId }: { botId: string }) {
  const { data: logs, isLoading, isError } = useListBotLogs(botId, { limit: 100 });

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <Skeleton className="h-8 w-48 mb-2" />
          <Skeleton className="h-4 w-72" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6].map(i => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-10 w-full" />)}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (isError || !logs) {
    return (
      <Card className="border-destructive/50 bg-destructive/10">
        <CardContent className="pt-6 text-center text-destructive">
          Failed to load logs.
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (logs.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Card className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-12 border-dashed">
        <FileText className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
        <CardTitle className="mb-2">No logs</CardTitle>
        <CardDescription className="text-center max-w-sm">
          No system logs have been generated yet.
        </CardDescription>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <Card>
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle>System Logs</CardTitle>
        <CardDescription>Recent system and activity logs.</CardDescription>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="rounded-md border bg-muted/20">
          <Table>
            <TableHeader>
              <TableRow>
                <TableHead className="w-32">Time</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="w-24">Level</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="w-32">Category</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Message</TableHead>
              </TableRow>
            </TableHeader>
            <TableBody>
              {logs.map(log => (
                <TableRow key={log.id} className="font-mono text-sm border-b-border/50">
                  <TableCell className="text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap">
                    {new Date(log.createdAt).toLocaleTimeString()}
                  </TableCell>
                  <TableCell>
                    <LogLevelBadge level={log.level} />
                  </TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="text-muted-foreground">{log.category}</TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="break-all">{log.message}</TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              ))}
            </TableBody>
          </Table>
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function LogLevelBadge({ level }: { level: string }) {
  const styles: Record<string, string> = {
    info: "text-blue-500 bg-blue-500/10 border-blue-500/20",
    warn: "text-amber-500 bg-amber-500/10 border-amber-500/20",
    error: "text-destructive bg-destructive/10 border-destructive/20",
    action: "text-emerald-500 bg-emerald-500/10 border-emerald-500/20",
  };

  return (
    <Badge variant="outline" className={`uppercase text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0 ${styles[level] || "bg-muted"}`}>
      {level}
    </Badge>
  );
}

// FILE: artifacts/bot-manager/src/components/bot/moderation-tab.tsx

import React from "react";
import { useListRecentModerationActions } from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
import { Shield } from "lucide-react";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";

export function ModerationTab({ botId }: { botId: string }) {
  const { data: actions, isLoading, isError } = useListRecentModerationActions(botId);

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <Skeleton className="h-8 w-48 mb-2" />
          <Skeleton className="h-4 w-72" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {[1, 2, 3, 4].map(i => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-16 w-full" />)}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (isError || !actions) {
    return (
      <Card className="border-destructive/50 bg-destructive/10">
        <CardContent className="pt-6 text-center text-destructive">
          Failed to load moderation actions.
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (actions.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Card className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-12 border-dashed">
        <Shield className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
        <CardTitle className="mb-2">No moderation actions</CardTitle>
        <CardDescription className="text-center max-w-sm">
          No moderation actions have been logged recently.
        </CardDescription>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <Card>
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle>Recent Moderation</CardTitle>
        <CardDescription>Recent moderation actions performed by this bot.</CardDescription>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="rounded-md border">
          <Table>
            <TableHeader>
              <TableRow>
                <TableHead>Action</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Target</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Reason</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Server</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Moderator</TableHead>
                <TableHead>Time</TableHead>
              </TableRow>
            </TableHeader>
            <TableBody>
              {actions.map(action => (
                <TableRow key={action.id}>
                  <TableCell>
                    <ActionBadge action={action.action} />
                  </TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="font-mono text-xs">{action.targetUser}</TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="text-muted-foreground max-w-xs truncate">{action.reason || "No reason provided"}</TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="text-muted-foreground">{action.guildName || "Unknown"}</TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{action.moderator}</TableCell>
                  <TableCell className="text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap">
                    {new Date(action.createdAt).toLocaleString()}
                  </TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              ))}
            </TableBody>
          </Table>
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function ActionBadge({ action }: { action: string }) {
  const styles: Record<string, string> = {
    ban: "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90",
    unban: "bg-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-500 hover:bg-emerald-500/30 border-transparent",
    kick: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-500 hover:bg-orange-500/30 border-transparent",
    timeout: "bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-500 hover:bg-yellow-500/30 border-transparent",
    untimeout: "bg-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-500 hover:bg-emerald-500/30 border-transparent",
    warn: "bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-500 hover:bg-amber-500/30 border-transparent",
    antiraid: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-500 hover:bg-purple-500/30 border-transparent",
    antinuke: "bg-rose-500/20 text-rose-500 hover:bg-rose-500/30 border-transparent",
  };

  return (
    <Badge variant="outline" className={`capitalize ${styles[action] || "bg-muted"}`}>
      {action}
    </Badge>
  );
}

// FILE: artifacts/bot-manager/src/components/bot/overview-tab.tsx
============================================================

import React from "react";
import { useGetBotStats, BotStats } from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
import { Activity, Users, ShieldAlert, TerminalSquare, Server, MessageSquare, Shield } from "lucide-react";
import { Area, AreaChart, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip, XAxis, YAxis } from "recharts";

export function OverviewTab({ botId }: { botId: string }) {
  const { data: stats, isLoading, isError } = useGetBotStats(botId);

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4">
          {[1, 2, 3, 4].map(i => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-32 w-full" />)}
        </div>
        <Skeleton className="h-[300px] w-full" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (isError || !stats) {
    return (
      <Card className="border-destructive/50 bg-destructive/10">
        <CardContent className="pt-6 text-center text-destructive">
          Failed to load bot statistics.
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4">
        <StatCard title="Total Guilds" value={stats.guilds} icon={Server} />
        <StatCard title="Total Members" value={stats.members} icon={Users} />
        <StatCard title="Commands Today" value={stats.commandsToday} icon={TerminalSquare} />
        <StatCard title="Threats Blocked (7d)" value={stats.threatsBlocked7d} icon={ShieldAlert} valueClass="text-emerald-500" />
        <StatCard title="Open Tickets" value={stats.ticketsOpen} icon={MessageSquare} />
        <StatCard title="Closed Tickets" value={stats.ticketsClosed} icon={Activity} />
        <StatCard title="Mod Actions (7d)" value={stats.moderationActions7d} icon={Shield} />
        <StatCard title="Uptime" value={formatUptime(stats.uptimeSeconds)} icon={Activity} />
      </div>

      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>Command Activity (7 Days)</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription>Daily command execution volume</CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="h-[300px] w-full">
            <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
              <AreaChart data={stats.commandActivity}>
                <defs>
                  <linearGradient id="colorCount" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                    <stop offset="5%" stopColor="hsl(var(--primary))" stopOpacity={0.3} />
                    <stop offset="95%" stopColor="hsl(var(--primary))" stopOpacity={0} />
                  </linearGradient>
                </defs>
                <XAxis dataKey="day" stroke="hsl(var(--muted-foreground))" fontSize={12} tickLine={false} axisLine={false} />
                <YAxis stroke="hsl(var(--muted-foreground))" fontSize={12} tickLine={false} axisLine={false} tickFormatter={(value) => `${value}`} />
                <Tooltip 
                  contentStyle={{ backgroundColor: "hsl(var(--card))", borderColor: "hsl(var(--border))", borderRadius: "8px" }}
                  itemStyle={{ color: "hsl(var(--foreground))" }}
                />
                <Area type="monotone" dataKey="count" stroke="hsl(var(--primary))" fillOpacity={1} fill="url(#colorCount)" strokeWidth={2} />
              </AreaChart>
            </ResponsiveContainer>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

function StatCard({ title, value, icon: Icon, valueClass }: { title: string; value: number | string; icon: React.ElementType; valueClass?: string }) {
  return (
    <Card>
      <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">{title}</CardTitle>
        <Icon className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className={`text-2xl font-bold ${valueClass || ""}`}>{value}</div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function formatUptime(seconds: number) {
  const d = Math.floor(seconds / (3600*24));
  const h = Math.floor(seconds % (3600*24) / 3600);
  const m = Math.floor(seconds % 3600 / 60);
  if (d > 0) return `${d}d ${h}h`;
  if (h > 0) return `${h}h ${m}m`;
  return `${m}m`;
}

import React, { useState } from "react";
import {
  useListBotGuilds,
  useListGuildChannels,
  useGetChannelMessages,

  useGetGuildConfig,

} from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback, AvatarImage } from "@/components/ui/avatar";

interface Guild {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  iconUrl?: string | null;
  memberCount: number;
}

function ChannelIcon({ type }: { type: string }) {
  if (type === "voice") return <Volume2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />;
  if (type === "announcement") return <Megaphone className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />;
  return <Hash className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />;
}

function timeAgo(iso: string) {
  const diff = Date.now() - new Date(iso).getTime();
  const mins = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
  if (mins < 1) return "just now";
  if (mins < 60) return `${mins}m ago`;
  const hrs = Math.floor(mins / 60);
  if (hrs < 24) return `${hrs}h ago`;
  return `${Math.floor(hrs / 24)}d ago`;
}

function ChatViewer({ botId, guildId }: { botId: string; guildId: string }) {
  const [selectedChannel, setSelectedChannel] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const { data: channels, isLoading: loadingChannels } = useListGuildChannels(botId, guildId);
  const textChannels = channels?.filter((c) => c.type === "text" || c.type === "announcement") ?? [];

  const { data: messages, isLoading: loadingMessages, refetch } = useGetChannelMessages(
    botId,
    guildId,
    selectedChannel ?? "skip",
    { limit: 50 },
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
    { query: { enabled: !!selectedChannel } as any },
  );

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full gap-3">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <div className="flex-1">
          {loadingChannels ? (
            <Skeleton className="h-9 w-full" />
          ) : (
            <Select value={selectedChannel ?? ""} onValueChange={setSelectedChannel}>
              <SelectTrigger>
                <SelectValue placeholder="Select a channel to view..." />
              </SelectTrigger>
              <SelectContent>
                {textChannels.map((ch) => (
                  <SelectItem key={ch.id} value={ch.id}>
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <ChannelIcon type={ch.type} />
                      {ch.name}
                      {ch.categoryName && (
                        <span className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">({ch.categoryName})</span>
                      )}
                    </span>
                  </SelectItem>
                ))}
              </SelectContent>
            </Select>
          )}
        </div>
        {selectedChannel && (
          <Button variant="outline" size="icon" onClick={() => refetch()} title="Refresh messages">
            <RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        )}
      </div>

      {!selectedChannel && (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-12 text-center text-muted-foreground">
          <MessageSquare className="h-10 w-10 mb-3 opacity-40" />
          <p className="text-sm">Pick a channel above to view its recent messages.</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {selectedChannel && (
        <ScrollArea className="flex-1 rounded-md border bg-muted/20 p-3 min-h-[300px]">
          {loadingMessages ? (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => (
                <div key={i} className="flex gap-2">
                  <Skeleton className="h-8 w-8 rounded-full shrink-0" />
                  <div className="space-y-1 flex-1">
                    <Skeleton className="h-3 w-24" />
                    <Skeleton className="h-4 w-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : messages && messages.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="space-y-4">
              {messages.map((msg) => (
                <div key={msg.id} className="flex gap-2.5 group">
                  <Avatar className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0">
                    <AvatarImage src={msg.authorAvatar ?? ""} />
                    <AvatarFallback className="text-xs">{msg.authorTag.slice(0, 2).toUpperCase()}</AvatarFallback>
                  </Avatar>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-baseline gap-2">
                      <span className="text-sm font-medium leading-none">{msg.authorTag}</span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{timeAgo(msg.timestamp)}</span>
                    </div>
                    {msg.content && (
                      <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-foreground/90 break-words whitespace-pre-wrap">
                        {msg.content}
                      </p>
                    )}
                    {msg.attachments.length > 0 && (
                      <div className="mt-1 flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                        {msg.attachments.map((url, i) => (
                          <a
                            key={i}
                            href={url}
                            target="_blank"
                            rel="noreferrer"
                            className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-primary hover:underline"
                          >
                            <Paperclip className="h-3 w-3" />
                            Attachment {i + 1}
                          </a>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">No messages found in this channel.</p>
          )}
        </ScrollArea>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function ServerSettingsPanel({
  botId,
  guildId,
  channels,
}: {
  botId: string;
  guildId: string;
  channels: Array<{ id: string; name: string; type: string }>;
}) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const { data: cfg, isLoading } = useGetGuildConfig(botId, guildId);
  const updateCfg = useUpdateGuildConfig();

  const textChannels = channels.filter((c) => c.type === "text" || c.type === "announcement");

  const [form, setForm] = React.useState({
    modLogChannelId: "",
    welcomeChannelId: "",
    welcomeMessage: "",
    ticketCategoryId: "",
    ticketSupportRoleId: "",
    aiChannelId: "",
    prefix: "",
  });

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (cfg) {
      setForm({
        modLogChannelId: cfg.modLogChannelId ?? "",
        welcomeChannelId: cfg.welcomeChannelId ?? "",
        welcomeMessage: cfg.welcomeMessage ?? "",
        ticketCategoryId: cfg.ticketCategoryId ?? "",
        ticketSupportRoleId: cfg.ticketSupportRoleId ?? "",
        aiChannelId: cfg.aiChannelId ?? "",
        prefix: cfg.prefix ?? "",
      });
    }
  }, [cfg]);

  const save = async () => {
    try {
      await updateCfg.mutateAsync({
        botId,
        guildId,
        data: {
          modLogChannelId: form.modLogChannelId || null,
          welcomeChannelId: form.welcomeChannelId || null,
          welcomeMessage: form.welcomeMessage || null,
          ticketCategoryId: form.ticketCategoryId || null,
          ticketSupportRoleId: form.ticketSupportRoleId || null,
          aiChannelId: form.aiChannelId || null,
          prefix: form.prefix || null,
        },
      });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: getGetGuildConfigQueryKey(botId, guildId) });
      toast({ title: "Server settings saved" });
    } catch {
      toast({ title: "Failed to save", variant: "destructive" });
    }
  };

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-16 w-full" />)}
      </div>
    );
  }

  const NONE = "__none__";

  const channelSelect = (
    value: string,
    onChange: (v: string) => void,
    placeholder: string,
  ) => (
    <Select
      value={value || NONE}
      onValueChange={(v) => onChange(v === NONE ? "" : v)}
    >
      <SelectTrigger>
        <SelectValue placeholder={placeholder} />
      </SelectTrigger>
      <SelectContent>
        <SelectItem value={NONE}>— None —</SelectItem>
        {textChannels.map((ch) => (
          <SelectItem key={ch.id} value={ch.id}>
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <Hash className="h-3 w-3" />
              {ch.name}
            </span>
          </SelectItem>
        ))}
      </SelectContent>
    </Select>
  );

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
        These settings override the global bot config for this server only.
      </p>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2">
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>Mod Log Channel</Label>
          {channelSelect(form.modLogChannelId, (v) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, modLogChannelId: v })), "Use global setting")}
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>Welcome Channel</Label>
          {channelSelect(form.welcomeChannelId, (v) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, welcomeChannelId: v })), "Use global setting")}
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>Ticket Category ID</Label>
          <Input
            placeholder="Category ID (paste from Discord)"
            value={form.ticketCategoryId}
            onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, ticketCategoryId: e.target.value }))}
          />
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>Ticket Support Role ID</Label>
          <Input
            placeholder="Role ID (paste from Discord)"
            value={form.ticketSupportRoleId}
            onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, ticketSupportRoleId: e.target.value }))}
          />
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>AI Chat Channel</Label>
          {channelSelect(form.aiChannelId, (v) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, aiChannelId: v })), "Use global setting")}
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label>Command Prefix</Label>
          <Input
            placeholder="Use global prefix"
            value={form.prefix}
            maxLength={3}
            onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, prefix: e.target.value }))}
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="space-y-1.5">
        <Label>Welcome Message</Label>
        <Input
          placeholder="Use global welcome message"
          value={form.welcomeMessage}
          onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, welcomeMessage: e.target.value }))}
        />
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Use {"{user}"} and {"{server}"} as placeholders.</p>
      </div>

      <Button onClick={save} disabled={updateCfg.isPending}>
        {updateCfg.isPending ? "Saving..." : "Save Server Settings"}
      </Button>
    </div>
  );
}

function InviteButton({ botId, guildId }: { botId: string; guildId: string }) {
  const [fetch, setFetch] = useState(false);
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
  const { data, isLoading } = useGetGuildInvite(botId, guildId, { query: { enabled: fetch } as any });

  const handleCopy = () => {
    if (data?.url) {
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(data.url);
      setCopied(true);
      setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
    }
  };

  if (!fetch) {
    return (
      <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={() => setFetch(true)}>
        <Link className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
        Get Invite
      </Button>
    );
  }

  if (isLoading) {
    return <Button variant="outline" size="sm" disabled><RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />Generating...</Button>;
  }

  if (!data?.url) {
    return <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Could not create invite (missing permission)</span>;
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <a
        href={data.url}
        target="_blank"
        rel="noreferrer"
        className="text-sm text-primary underline underline-offset-2 truncate max-w-[220px]"
      >
        {data.url}
      </a>
      <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-7 w-7" onClick={handleCopy}>
        {copied ? <Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-500" /> : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
      </Button>
    </div>
  );
}

function NukePanel({ botId, guildId, guildName }: { botId: string; guildId: string; guildName: string }) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const nuke = useNukeGuild();
  const [banMembers, setBanMembers] = useState(false);
  const [deleteChannels, setDeleteChannels] = useState(false);
  const [channelNames, setChannelNames] = useState("");
  const [result, setResult] = useState<{ banned: number; deletedChannels: number; createdChannels: number; errors: string[] } | null>(null);

  const channelList = channelNames
    .split("\n")
    .map((n) => n.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);

  const execute = async () => {
    try {
      setResult(null);
      const res = await nuke.mutateAsync({
        botId,
        guildId,
        data: {
          banMembers,
          deleteChannels,
          createChannels: channelList,
        },
      });
      setResult(res);
      toast({ title: "Nuke executed", description: `Banned: ${res.banned} · Deleted channels: ${res.deletedChannels} · Created: ${res.createdChannels}` });
    } catch {
      toast({ title: "Nuke failed", variant: "destructive" });
    }
  };

  const nothingSelected = !banMembers && !deleteChannels && channelList.length === 0;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="rounded-lg border border-destructive/40 bg-destructive/10 p-4 flex gap-3">
        <AlertTriangle className="h-5 w-5 text-destructive shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
        <div className="space-y-1">
          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-destructive">Danger zone — irreversible actions</p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            These actions run immediately and cannot be undone. The bot needs Administrator permissions in <strong>{guildName}</strong> for all options to work.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="space-y-4">
        <div className="flex items-start gap-3 rounded-lg border p-4">
          <Checkbox
            id="ban-members"
            checked={banMembers}
            onCheckedChange={(v) => setBanMembers(!!v)}
            className="mt-0.5"
          />
          <div>
            <label htmlFor="ban-members" className="text-sm font-medium cursor-pointer">Ban all members</label>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
              Mass-bans every non-bot member (except the server owner). Runs in parallel for maximum speed.
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-start gap-3 rounded-lg border p-4">
          <Checkbox
            id="delete-channels"
            checked={deleteChannels}
            onCheckedChange={(v) => setDeleteChannels(!!v)}
            className="mt-0.5"
          />
          <div>
            <label htmlFor="delete-channels" className="text-sm font-medium cursor-pointer">Delete all channels</label>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
              Deletes every channel, category, and voice channel in the server.
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="space-y-2">
          <label className="text-sm font-medium">Create channels (one name per line)</label>
          <Textarea
            placeholder={"general\nannouncements\nrules\nbot-commands"}
            value={channelNames}
            onChange={(e) => setChannelNames(e.target.value)}
            rows={5}
            className="font-mono text-sm resize-none"
          />
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            Channel names are auto-formatted to lowercase with hyphens. Leave empty to skip creation.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {result && (
        <div className="rounded-lg border border-border bg-muted/30 p-4 space-y-2">
          <p className="text-sm font-semibold">Nuke complete</p>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 text-center">
            <div className="rounded border p-2">
              <p className="text-xl font-bold">{result.banned}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Banned</p>
            </div>
            <div className="rounded border p-2">
              <p className="text-xl font-bold">{result.deletedChannels}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Deleted</p>
            </div>
            <div className="rounded border p-2">
              <p className="text-xl font-bold">{result.createdChannels}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Created</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          {result.errors.length > 0 && (
            <div className="space-y-1 mt-2">
              <p className="text-xs font-medium text-destructive">{result.errors.length} error(s):</p>
              {result.errors.slice(0, 5).map((e, i) => (
                <p key={i} className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                  <X className="h-3 w-3 text-destructive" /> {e}
                </p>
              ))}
              {result.errors.length > 5 && (
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">…and {result.errors.length - 5} more</p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      <AlertDialog>
        <AlertDialogTrigger asChild>
          <Button
            variant="destructive"
            className="w-full gap-2"
            disabled={nothingSelected || nuke.isPending}
          >
            <Skull className="h-4 w-4" />
            {nuke.isPending ? "Nuking…" : "Execute Nuke"}
          </Button>
        </AlertDialogTrigger>
        <AlertDialogContent>
          <AlertDialogHeader>
            <AlertDialogTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-destructive">
              <Skull className="h-5 w-5" /> Confirm nuke of {guildName}
            </AlertDialogTitle>
            <AlertDialogDescription className="space-y-2">
              <span className="block">You are about to run the following on <strong>{guildName}</strong>:</span>
              {banMembers && <span className="block">• Ban all members</span>}
              {deleteChannels && <span className="block">• Delete all channels</span>}
              {channelList.length > 0 && (
                <span className="block">• Create {channelList.length} channel(s): {channelList.map((n) => `#${n}`).join(", ")}</span>
              )}
              <span className="block font-semibold text-destructive mt-2">This cannot be undone.</span>
            </AlertDialogDescription>
          </AlertDialogHeader>
          <AlertDialogFooter>
            <AlertDialogCancel>Cancel</AlertDialogCancel>
            <AlertDialogAction
              onClick={execute}
              className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90"
            >
              Yes, Nuke It
            </AlertDialogAction>
          </AlertDialogFooter>
        </AlertDialogContent>
      </AlertDialog>
    </div>
  );
}

function ServerDialog({
  botId,
  guild,
  open,
  onClose,
}: {
  botId: string;
  guild: Guild;
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}) {
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
  const { data: channels, isLoading: loadingChannels } = useListGuildChannels(botId, guild.id, { query: { enabled: open } as any });

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={(v) => !v && onClose()}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-3xl w-full h-[85vh] flex flex-col p-0 gap-0">
        <DialogHeader className="px-6 pt-5 pb-3 border-b">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <Avatar className="h-10 w-10">
              <AvatarImage src={guild.iconUrl ?? ""} alt={guild.name} />
              <AvatarFallback>{guild.name.slice(0, 2).toUpperCase()}</AvatarFallback>
            </Avatar>
            <div>
              <DialogTitle className="text-lg">{guild.name}</DialogTitle>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                <Users className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                {guild.memberCount.toLocaleString()} members · ID: {guild.id}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </DialogHeader>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 px-6 py-3 border-b">
          <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Invite link:</span>
          <InviteButton botId={botId} guildId={guild.id} />
        </div>

        <Tabs defaultValue="channels" className="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
          <TabsList className="mx-6 mt-3 w-fit">
            <TabsTrigger value="channels">Channels</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="chat">View Chat</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="settings">Server Settings</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="nuke" className="text-destructive data-[state=active]:text-destructive">
              <Skull className="h-3.5 w-3.5 mr-1.5" />Nuke
            </TabsTrigger>
          </TabsList>

          <TabsContent value="channels" className="flex-1 overflow-hidden px-6 pb-6 mt-3">
            <ScrollArea className="h-full rounded-md border">
              {loadingChannels ? (
                <div className="p-4 space-y-2">
                  {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-8 w-full" />)}
                </div>
              ) : channels && channels.length > 0 ? (
                <div className="p-2">
                  {Object.entries(
                    channels.reduce<Record<string, typeof channels>>((acc, ch) => {
                      const cat = ch.categoryName ?? "Uncategorized";
                      if (!acc[cat]) acc[cat] = [];
                      acc[cat].push(ch);
                      return acc;
                    }, {}),
                  ).map(([cat, chs]) => (
                    <div key={cat} className="mb-3">
                      <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider px-2 py-1">
                        {cat}
                      </p>
                      {chs.map((ch) => (
                        <div
                          key={ch.id}
                          className="flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 rounded hover:bg-muted/50"
                        >
                          <ChannelIcon type={ch.type} />
                          <span className="text-sm">{ch.name}</span>
                          <span className="ml-auto font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{ch.id}</span>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">No channels found.</p>
              )}
            </ScrollArea>
          </TabsContent>

          <TabsContent value="chat" className="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden px-6 pb-6 mt-3">
            <ChatViewer botId={botId} guildId={guild.id} />
          </TabsContent>

          <TabsContent value="settings" className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-6 mt-3">
            {loadingChannels ? (
              <div className="space-y-3">
                {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-14 w-full" />)}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <ServerSettingsPanel
                botId={botId}
                guildId={guild.id}
                channels={channels ?? []}
              />
            )}
          </TabsContent>

          <TabsContent value="nuke" className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-6 pb-6 mt-3">
            <NukePanel botId={botId} guildId={guild.id} guildName={guild.name} />
          </TabsContent>
        </Tabs>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}

export function ServersTab({ botId }: { botId: string }) {
  const { data: guilds, isLoading, isError } = useListBotGuilds(botId);
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<Guild | null>(null);

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <Skeleton className="h-8 w-48 mb-2" />
          <Skeleton className="h-4 w-72" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-20 w-full" />)}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (isError || !guilds) {
    return (
      <Card className="border-destructive/50 bg-destructive/10">
        <CardContent className="pt-6 text-center text-destructive">
          Failed to load servers.
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  if (guilds.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Card className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-12 border-dashed">
        <Server className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
        <CardTitle className="mb-2">No servers yet</CardTitle>
        <CardDescription className="text-center max-w-sm">
          This bot hasn't been added to any servers. Generate an invite link using the bot's OAuth2 URL from the Discord Developer Portal.
        </CardDescription>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <>
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>Servers ({guilds.length})</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription>
            Click a server to view its channels, read chat, get an invite link, or configure per-server settings.
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {guilds.map((guild) => (
              <div
                key={guild.id}
                className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border bg-card hover:bg-muted/40 cursor-pointer transition-colors"
                onClick={() => setSelected(guild)}
              >
                <Avatar className="h-10 w-10 shrink-0">
                  <AvatarImage src={guild.iconUrl ?? ""} alt={guild.name} />
                  <AvatarFallback>{guild.name.slice(0, 2).toUpperCase()}</AvatarFallback>
                </Avatar>
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="font-medium truncate">{guild.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-mono">{guild.id}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 shrink-0">
                  <Badge variant="secondary" className="gap-1">
                    <Users className="h-3 w-3" />
                    {guild.memberCount.toLocaleString()}
                  </Badge>
                  <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setSelected(guild); }}>
                    <Settings2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 mr-1.5" />
                    Manage
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {selected && (
        <ServerDialog
          botId={botId}
          guild={selected}
          open={!!selected}
          onClose={() => setSelected(null)}
        />
      )}
    </>
  );
}

import React from "react";
import { useGetBotConfig, useUpdateBotConfig, getGetBotConfigQueryKey } from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardFooter } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Form, FormControl, FormDescription, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage } from "@/components/ui/form";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
import * as z from "zod";
import { useQueryClient, useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
import { Shield, MessageSquare, Ticket, Settings as SettingsIcon, AlertTriangle, Filter, Info, Terminal, Palette, FileText, UserCog, Send, Hash } from "lucide-react";
import { useSendBotEmbed, useSendBotMessage } from "@workspace/api-client-react";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";

type AllChannelEntry = { guildId: string; guildName: string; channelId: string; channelName: string };

function useAllChannels(botId: string) {
  return useQuery<AllChannelEntry[]>({
    queryKey: ["all-channels", botId],
    queryFn: async () => {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/bots/${botId}/all-channels`);
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load channels");
      return res.json() as Promise<AllChannelEntry[]>;
    },
    staleTime: 30_000,
  });
}

function ChannelSelect({
  botId,
  value,
  onChange,
  placeholder,
}: {
  botId: string;
  value: string;
  onChange: (v: string) => void;
  placeholder: string;
}) {
  const NONE = "__none__";
  const { data: channels = [], isLoading } = useAllChannels(botId);

  const grouped = React.useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, { guildName: string; channels: AllChannelEntry[] }>();
    for (const ch of channels) {
      if (!map.has(ch.guildId)) map.set(ch.guildId, { guildName: ch.guildName, channels: [] });
      map.get(ch.guildId)!.channels.push(ch);
    }
    return [...map.values()];
  }, [channels]);

  const selected = channels.find((c) => c.channelId === value);

  return (
    <Select value={value || NONE} onValueChange={(v) => onChange(v === NONE ? "" : v)} disabled={isLoading}>
      <SelectTrigger>
        <SelectValue placeholder={isLoading ? "Loading channels…" : placeholder}>
          {selected ? (
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <Hash className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
              <span className="truncate">{selected.channelName}</span>
              <span className="text-muted-foreground text-xs ml-1 shrink-0">({selected.guildName})</span>
            </span>
          ) : null}
        </SelectValue>
      </SelectTrigger>
      <SelectContent>
        <ScrollArea className="max-h-60">
          <SelectItem value={NONE}>— None —</SelectItem>
          {grouped.map(({ guildName, channels: gChans }) => (
            <React.Fragment key={guildName}>
              <div className="px-2 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
                {guildName}
              </div>
              {gChans.map((ch) => (
                <SelectItem key={ch.channelId} value={ch.channelId}>
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                    <Hash className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
                    {ch.channelName}
                  </span>
                </SelectItem>
              ))}
            </React.Fragment>
          ))}
        </ScrollArea>
      </SelectContent>
    </Select>
  );
}

const configSchema = z.object({
  welcomeEnabled: z.boolean(),
  welcomeChannelId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  welcomeMessage: z.string(),
  ticketsEnabled: z.boolean(),
  ticketCategoryId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  ticketSupportRoleId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  afkEnabled: z.boolean(),
  aiChatEnabled: z.boolean(),
  aiChannelId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  aiPersonality: z.string(),
  antiNukeEnabled: z.boolean(),
  antiRaidEnabled: z.boolean(),
  antiRaidJoinThreshold: z.coerce.number().min(2).max(50),
  antiRaidJoinWindowSec: z.coerce.number().min(5).max(300),
  modLogChannelId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
  automodEnabled: z.boolean(),
  automodBadWords: z.string(),
  automodBlockLinks: z.boolean(),
  automodLinkWhitelist: z.string(),
  automodSpamEnabled: z.boolean(),
  automodSpamMaxMessages: z.coerce.number().min(2).max(50),
  automodSpamWindowSec: z.coerce.number().min(2).max(60),
  automodAction: z.enum(["delete", "warn", "timeout", "kick"]),
  prefixEnabled: z.boolean(),
  prefix: z.string().min(1).max(3),
  ticketPanelTitle: z.string(),
  ticketPanelDescription: z.string(),
  ticketPanelButtonLabel: z.string(),
  embedFooter: z.string(),
  embedColor: z.string(),
  messageLogEnabled: z.boolean(),
  roleLimitEnabled: z.boolean(),
  roleLimitMax: z.coerce.number().min(1).max(20),
  requiredRoleEnabled: z.boolean(),
  requiredRoleId: z.string().nullable(),
  superOwnerId: z.string().nullable(),
  nukeCommandEnabled: z.boolean(),
  nukeCommandPrefix: z.string().min(1).max(5),
  nukeCommandMessages: z.string(),
});

type ConfigFormValues = z.infer<typeof configSchema>;

export function SettingsTab({ botId }: { botId: string }) {
  const { data: config, isLoading, isError } = useGetBotConfig(botId);
  const updateConfig = useUpdateBotConfig();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const { toast } = useToast();

  const form = useForm<ConfigFormValues>({
    resolver: zodResolver(configSchema as any),
    defaultValues: {
      welcomeEnabled: false,
      welcomeChannelId: "",
      welcomeMessage: "Welcome to the server, {user}!",
      ticketsEnabled: false,
      ticketCategoryId: "",
      ticketSupportRoleId: "",
      afkEnabled: false,
      aiChatEnabled: false,
      aiChannelId: "",
      aiPersonality: "You are a helpful assistant.",
      antiNukeEnabled: false,
      antiRaidEnabled: false,
      antiRaidJoinThreshold: 5,
      antiRaidJoinWindowSec: 60,
      modLogChannelId: "",
      automodEnabled: false,
      automodBadWords: "",
      automodBlockLinks: false,
      automodLinkWhitelist: "",
      automodSpamEnabled: false,
      automodSpamMaxMessages: 5,
      automodSpamWindowSec: 5,
      automodAction: "delete",
      prefixEnabled: true,
      prefix: "+",
      ticketPanelTitle: "Need help?",
      ticketPanelDescription: "Click the button below to open a private support ticket with our staff.",
      ticketPanelButtonLabel: "Open Ticket",
      embedFooter: "Coded by Montaser",
      embedColor: "#5865F2",
      messageLogEnabled: false,
      roleLimitEnabled: false,
      roleLimitMax: 2,
      requiredRoleEnabled: false,
      requiredRoleId: "",
      superOwnerId: "",
      nukeCommandEnabled: false,
      nukeCommandPrefix: ".",
      nukeCommandMessages: "",
    },
  });

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (config) {
      form.reset({
        welcomeEnabled: config.welcomeEnabled,
        welcomeChannelId: config.welcomeChannelId || "",
        welcomeMessage: config.welcomeMessage,
        ticketsEnabled: config.ticketsEnabled,
        ticketCategoryId: config.ticketCategoryId || "",
        ticketSupportRoleId: config.ticketSupportRoleId || "",
        afkEnabled: config.afkEnabled,
        aiChatEnabled: config.aiChatEnabled,
        aiChannelId: config.aiChannelId || "",
        aiPersonality: config.aiPersonality,
        antiNukeEnabled: config.antiNukeEnabled,
        antiRaidEnabled: config.antiRaidEnabled,
        antiRaidJoinThreshold: config.antiRaidJoinThreshold,
        antiRaidJoinWindowSec: config.antiRaidJoinWindowSec,
        modLogChannelId: config.modLogChannelId || "",
        automodEnabled: config.automodEnabled,
        automodBadWords: config.automodBadWords,
        automodBlockLinks: config.automodBlockLinks,
        automodLinkWhitelist: config.automodLinkWhitelist,
        automodSpamEnabled: config.automodSpamEnabled,
        automodSpamMaxMessages: config.automodSpamMaxMessages,
        automodSpamWindowSec: config.automodSpamWindowSec,
        automodAction: config.automodAction as "delete" | "warn" | "timeout" | "kick",
        prefixEnabled: config.prefixEnabled,
        prefix: config.prefix,
        ticketPanelTitle: config.ticketPanelTitle,
        ticketPanelDescription: config.ticketPanelDescription,
        ticketPanelButtonLabel: config.ticketPanelButtonLabel,
        embedFooter: config.embedFooter,
        embedColor: config.embedColor,
        messageLogEnabled: config.messageLogEnabled,
        roleLimitEnabled: config.roleLimitEnabled,
        roleLimitMax: config.roleLimitMax,
        requiredRoleEnabled: config.requiredRoleEnabled,
        requiredRoleId: config.requiredRoleId ?? "",
        superOwnerId: config.superOwnerId ?? "",
        nukeCommandEnabled: config.nukeCommandEnabled,
        nukeCommandPrefix: config.nukeCommandPrefix || ".",
        nukeCommandMessages: config.nukeCommandMessages || "",
      });
    }
  }, [config, form]);

  const onSubmit = async (data: ConfigFormValues) => {
    try {
      const payload = {
        ...data,
        requiredRoleId: data.requiredRoleId && data.requiredRoleId.trim() ? data.requiredRoleId.trim() : null,
        superOwnerId: data.superOwnerId && data.superOwnerId.trim() ? data.superOwnerId.trim() : null,
      };
      await updateConfig.mutateAsync({ botId, data: payload });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: getGetBotConfigQueryKey(botId) });
      toast({ title: "Configuration saved", description: "Bot settings have been updated successfully." });
    } catch (error) {
      toast({ title: "Failed to save", description: "There was an error updating the configuration.", variant: "destructive" });
    }
  };

  if (isLoading) {
    return <Skeleton className="h-[600px] w-full" />;
  }

  if (isError || !config) {
    return <div className="text-destructive text-center py-8">Failed to load configuration.</div>;
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <Card className="border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/5">
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-amber-300">
            <Info className="h-5 w-5" /> One-time Discord setup
          </CardTitle>
          <CardDescription className="text-amber-200/80">
            For welcomes, AFK, AI chat, and automod to work, the bot needs the privileged intents enabled in Discord. Open the
            {" "}
            <a
              href="https://discord.com/developers/applications"
              target="_blank"
              rel="noreferrer"
              className="underline font-medium"
            >
              Discord Developer Portal
            </a>
            , pick your application, go to <span className="font-medium">Bot</span>, and turn on
            {" "}<span className="font-medium">Server Members Intent</span> and
            {" "}<span className="font-medium">Message Content Intent</span>. Then click Start again here.
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
      </Card>

      <Form {...form}>
        <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
          
          <Card>
            <CardHeader>
              <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <Shield className="h-5 w-5 text-primary" /> Moderation & Protection
              </CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-6">
              <FormField control={form.control} name="antiNukeEnabled" render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                  <div className="space-y-0.5">
                    <FormLabel className="text-base">Anti-Nuke</FormLabel>
                    <FormDescription>Prevent mass bans, kicks, and channel deletions.</FormDescription>
                  </div>
                  <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={field.onChange} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
              )} />

              <FormField control={form.control} name="antiRaidEnabled" render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                  <div className="space-y-0.5">
                    <FormLabel className="text-base">Anti-Raid</FormLabel>
                    <FormDescription>Prevent mass user joins in a short period.</FormDescription>
                  </div>
                  <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={field.onChange} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
              )} />

              {form.watch("antiRaidEnabled") && (
                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 pl-4 border-l-2 border-primary/20 ml-2">
                  <FormField control={form.control} name="antiRaidJoinThreshold" render={({ field }) => (
                    <FormItem>
                      <FormLabel>Join Threshold</FormLabel>
                      <FormControl><Input type="number" {...field} /></FormControl>
                      <FormDescription>Max joins allowed.</FormDescription>
                    </FormItem>
                  )} />
                  <FormField control={form.control} name="antiRaidJoinWindowSec" render={({ field }) => (
                    <FormItem>
                      <FormLabel>Time Window (seconds)</FormLabel>
                      <FormControl><Input type="number" {...field} /></FormControl>
                      <FormDescription>Time period for joins.</FormDescription>
                    </FormItem>
                  )} />
                </div>
              )}

              <FormField control={form.control} name="modLogChannelId" render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem>
                  <FormLabel>Mod Log Channel</FormLabel>
                  <FormControl>
                    <ChannelSelect
                      botId={botId}
                      value={field.value || ""}
                      onChange={field.onChange}
                      placeholder="Select a channel…"
                    />
                  </FormControl>
                  <FormDescription>Where to send moderation action logs.</FormDescription>
                </FormItem>
              )} />
            </CardContent>
          </Card>

          <Card>
            <CardHeader>
              <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <Ticket className="h-5 w-5 text-primary" /> Tickets System
              </CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-6">
              <FormField control={form.control} name="ticketsEnabled" render={({ field }) => (
                <FormItem className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between rounded-lg border p-4">
                  <div className="space-y-0.5">
                    <FormLabel className="text-base">Enable Tickets</FormLabel>
                    <FormDescription>Allow users to open support tickets.</FormDescription>
                  </div>
                  <FormControl><Switch checked={field.value} onCheckedChange={field.onChange} /></FormControl>
                </FormItem>
              )} />
              
              {form.watch("ticketsEnabled") && (
                <div className="space-y-4 pl-4 border-l-2 border-primary/20 ml-2">
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                    <FormField control={form.control} name="ticketCategoryId" render={({ field }) => (
                      <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>Ticket Category ID</FormLabel>

                      </FormItem>
                    )} />
                    <FormField control={form.control} name="ticketSupportRoleId" render={({ field }) => (
                      <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>Support Role ID</FormLabel>
                        <FormControl><Input placeholder="Role ID..." {...field} value={field.value || ""} /></FormControl>
                      </FormItem>
                    )} />
                  </div>
                  <Separator />
                  <div>
                    <h4 className="font-medium text-sm mb-3">Ticket Panel Embed</h4>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-4">
                      In any channel, run <code className="text-foreground bg-muted px-1 py-0.5 rounded">/ticket-panel</code> to post this embed with the Open Ticket button.

                    <div className="space-y-4">

Type <code className="text-foreground bg-muted px-1 py-0.5 rounded">+help</code> in chat for the full list.
